NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
SONY PICTURES IMAGEWORKS INDIA
In the matter of the Companies Act, 1956
and
In the matter of Section 485 (1) of the Companies Act, 1956
and
Sony Pictures Image Works India Private Limited
Flat F1 1st Floor, Mount Chambers, 758 Mount Road, Chennai-600 002.
Notice is hereby given that the members of Sony Pictures Imageworks India Private Limited (“Company”) at an
Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on January 31, 2017 at 10.00 a.m. at Flat-F, 1st Floor, Mount Chambers
758, Mount Road, Chennai-600 002, India have passed the following resolutions to wind up the Company voluntarily.
“RESOLVED THAT in terms of Provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the Company be and is
hereby voluntarily wound up subject to the necessary approvals/consents of the Registrar of Companies, Official Liquidator,
the Hon’ble Jurisdictional High Court/National Company Law Tribunal and such other authorities as may be necessary.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT a declaration and the statement on estimated realizable value of assets and liabilities
as required under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956 in Form 149 of Companies Court Rules, 1959 as on March 31,
2016 taken on oath by Mr. Peter Louis Jensen and Mr. Michael James Nazitto, representing a majority of the Directors of
the Company, be and are hereby confirmed, approved and adopted by this meeting to be presented to the Hon’ble
Jurisdictional High Court/National Company Law Tribunal or such other authorities, as may be required.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT for the purpose of giving effect to this resolution, any of the Directors be and are hereby
authorized to do all such other acts, deeds, matters and things incidental to make the resolution effective.”
By order of the Board.
Chennai,
13th February 2017.

Peter Jensen,
Director.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
